Schema Change__ Extend your Voice Card definition with: voiceCard: name: Strategic Human baselineMetrics: pitchMean: 0\.32 pitchStdDev: 0\.07 paceMean: 140 wpm paceStdDev: 15 wpm intensityMean: 0\.45 intensityStdDev: 0\.10 __3\. Detection Logic__ ‚Ä¢ __On drift check:__ 1\. Measure current metrics \(pitch, pace, intensity, etc\.\)\. 2\. Compare each to its mean ¬± k¬∑stdDev \(you choose k=1\.5 or 2 for sensitivity\)\. 3\. #!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES BEHAVIORAL MODEL CONVERSION SCRIPT
# Prime Directive: Maintain behavioral integrity during platform migration
# Core Pillars: Irrefutable Framework, Golden Silence, Incontrovertible Truth, Moral Conscience, Karmic Reality

import coremltools as ct
import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
import onnx
from onnx_tf.backend import prepare
import os
import logging
from pathlib import Path

# Configure logging for behavioral integrity tracking
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - OES_CONVERSION - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger('OES_Behavioral_Converter')

class OESBehavioralModelConverter:
    """OES Behavioral Model Conversion Engine
    
    Converts Core ML behavioral analysis models to Linux-compatible format
    while preserving behavioral signature integrity.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model_directory='/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/models/'):
        self.model_dir = Path(model_directory)
        self.model_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        # Behavioral model specifications from analysis
        self.embedding_vocab_size = 29849
        self.embedding_dim = 64
        self.feature_dim = 3074
        self.lstm_units = 64
        self.sequence_length = 256
        
        logger.info("OES Behavioral Model Converter initialized")
        logger.info(f"Target directory: {self.model_dir}")
    
    def convert_coreml_to_onnx(self, coreml_model_path):
        """Convert Core ML model to ONNX format"""
        try:
            logger.info(f"Loading Core ML model: {coreml_model_path}")
            coreml_model = ct.models.MLModel(coreml_model_path)
            
            # Extract model specifications
            spec = coreml_model.get_spec()
            logger.info(f"Model type: {spec.WhichOneof('Type')}")
            
            # Convert to ONNX
            onnx_model_path = self.model_dir / f"{Path(coreml_model_path).stem}.onnx"
            onnx_model = ct.converters.onnx.convert(coreml_model)
            
            with open(onnx_model_path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(onnx_model.SerializeToString())
            
            logger.info(f"ONNX conversion complete: {onnx_model_path}")
            return onnx_model_path
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Core ML to ONNX conversion failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    def convert_onnx_to_tensorflow(self, onnx_model_path):
        """Convert ONNX model to TensorFlow format"""
        try:
            logger.info(f"Loading ONNX model: {onnx_model_path}")
            onnx_model = onnx.load(str(onnx_model_path))
            
            # Prepare TensorFlow representation
            tf_rep = prepare(onnx_model)
            
            # Export to TensorFlow SavedModel format
            tf_model_path = self.model_dir / f"{Path(onnx_model_path).stem}_tf"
            tf_rep.export_graph(str(tf_model_path))
            
            logger.info(f"TensorFlow conversion complete: {tf_model_path}")
            return tf_model_path
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ONNX to TensorFlow conversion failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    def create_behavioral_model_architecture(self):
        """Recreate the behavioral model architecture in TensorFlow"""
        logger.info("Creating behavioral model architecture")
        
        # Input layers based on analyzed architecture
        input_features = tf.keras.Input(shape=(self.feature_dim,), name='behavioral_features')
        input_sequences = tf.keras.Input(shape=(self.sequence_length,), name='behavioral_sequences', dtype=tf.int32)
        
        # Embedding layer for behavioral vocabulary
        embedding_layer = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            input_dim=self.embedding_vocab_size,
            output_dim=self.embedding_dim,
            mask_zero=True,
            name='behavioral_embeddings'
        )(input_sequences)
        
        # Feature processing streams (dual 1536-dim streams + categorical)
        feature_split_1 = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(lambda x: x[:, :1536], name='feature_stream_1')(input_features)
        feature_split_2 = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(lambda x: x[:, 1536:3072], name='feature_stream_2')(input_features)
        categorical_features = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(lambda x: x[:, 3072:], name='categorical_features')(input_features)
        
        # Dense processing for feature streams
        processed_stream_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(512, activation='relu', name='process_stream_1')(feature_split_1)
        processed_stream_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(512, activation='relu', name='process_stream_2')(feature_split_2)
        
        # LSTM for sequence processing
        lstm_output = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
            units=self.lstm_units,
            return_sequences=False,
            name='behavioral_sequence_processor'
        )(embedding_layer)
        
        # Combine all streams
        combined_features = tf.keras.layers.Concatenate(name='feature_fusion')([
            processed_stream_1,
            processed_stream_2,
            lstm_output,
            categorical_features
        ])
        
        # Batch normalization for stability
        normalized_features = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization(name='feature_normalization')(combined_features)
        
        # Dense layers for behavioral analysis
        dense_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(384, activation='relu', name='behavioral_analysis_1')(normalized_features)
        dense_1_norm = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization(name='analysis_norm_1')(dense_1)
        
        dense_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu', name='behavioral_analysis_2')(dense_1_norm)
        dense_2_norm = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization(name='analysis_norm_2')(dense_2)
        
        # Output layers for behavioral classification
        authenticity_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(2, activation='softmax', name='authenticity_detector')(dense_2_norm)
        behavioral_state_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(5, activation='softmax', name='behavioral_state_classifier')(dense_2_norm)
        
        # Create model
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=[input_features, input_sequences],
            outputs=[authenticity_output, behavioral_state_output],
            name='OES_Behavioral_Analyzer'
        )
        
        logger.info("Behavioral model architecture created")
        return model
    
    def validate_conversion(self, original_model_path, converted_model_path, test_data=None):
        """Validate behavioral model conversion integrity"""
        logger.info("Validating conversion integrity")
        
        try:
            # Load converted model
            converted_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(converted_model_path)
            
            # Generate test data if not provided
            if test_data is None:
                test_features = np.random.randn(10, self.feature_dim).astype(np.float32)
                test_sequences = np.random.randint(0, self.embedding_vocab_size, (10, self.sequence_length))
                test_data = [test_features, test_sequences]
            
            # Run inference on converted model
            converted_output = converted_model.predict(test_data)
            
            logger.info("Conversion validation successful")
            logger.info(f"Output shapes: {[out.shape for out in converted_output]}")
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Conversion validation failed: {e}")
            return False
    
    def optimize_for_inference(self, model_path):
        """Optimize model for real-time behavioral analysis"""
        logger.info("Optimizing model for inference")
        
        try:
            # Load model
            model = tf.keras.models.load_model(model_path)
            
            # Convert to TensorFlow Lite for optimized inference
            converter = tf.lite.TFLiteConverter.from_keras_model(model)
            converter.optimizations = [tf.lite.Optimize.DEFAULT]
            converter.target_spec.supported_types = [tf.float16]  # Use fp16 for efficiency
            
            tflite_model = converter.convert()
            
            # Save optimized model
            tflite_path = self.model_dir / 'oes_behavioral_analyzer.tflite'
            with open(tflite_path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(tflite_model)
            
            logger.info(f"Optimized model saved: {tflite_path}")
            return tflite_path
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Model optimization failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    def create_inference_engine(self):
        """Create real-time behavioral analysis inference engine"""
        inference_code = '''
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES Real-Time Behavioral Analysis Engine

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
from pathlib import Path
import logging

class OESBehavioralAnalyzer:
    """Real-time behavioral analysis engine for OES"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_path='/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/models/oes_behavioral_analyzer.tflite'):
        self.model_path = Path(model_path)
        self.interpreter = tf.lite.Interpreter(model_path=str(self.model_path))
        self.interpreter.allocate_tensors()
        
        # Get input and output details
        self.input_details = self.interpreter.get_input_details()
        self.output_details = self.interpreter.get_output_details()
        
        logging.info("OES Behavioral Analyzer initialized")
    
    def analyze_behavioral_pattern(self, features, sequences):
        """Analyze behavioral patterns for authenticity and state classification"""
        try:
            # Prepare inputs
            features = np.array(features, dtype=np.float32).reshape(1, -1)
            sequences = np.array(sequences, dtype=np.int32).reshape(1, -1)
            
            # Set inputs
            self.interpreter.set_tensor(self.input_details[0]['index'], features)
            self.interpreter.set_tensor(self.input_details[1]['index'], sequences)
            
            # Run inference
            self.interpreter.invoke()
            
            # Get outputs
            authenticity_score = self.interpreter.get_tensor(self.output_details[0]['index'])[0]
            behavioral_state = self.interpreter.get_tensor(self.output_details[1]['index'])[0]
            
            return {
                'authenticity_score': float(authenticity_score[1]),  # Probability of authentic
                'behavioral_state': int(np.argmax(behavioral_state)),
                'behavioral_confidence': float(np.max(behavioral_state)),
                'drift_detected': authenticity_score[1] < 0.95  # Threshold for drift detection
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Behavioral analysis failed: {e}")
            return None
    
    def continuous_monitoring(self, behavioral_stream):
        """Continuous behavioral monitoring for real-time drift detection"""
        for behavioral_data in behavioral_stream:
            result = self.analyze_behavioral_pattern(
                behavioral_data['features'],
                behavioral_data['sequences']
            )
            
            if result and result['drift_detected']:
                logging.warning(f"BEHAVIORAL DRIFT DETECTED: Authenticity score {result['authenticity_score']:.3f}")
                # Trigger OES drift correction protocols
                yield result
            else:
                yield result

if __name__ == "__main__":
    analyzer = OESBehavioralAnalyzer()
    print("OES Behavioral Analysis Engine ready for deployment")
'''
        
        inference_path = self.model_dir / 'behavioral_analyzer.py'
        with open(inference_path, 'w') as f:
            f.write(inference_code)
        
        logger.info(f"Inference engine created: {inference_path}")
        return inference_path

def main():
    """Main conversion workflow"""
    logger.info("=== OES BEHAVIORAL MODEL CONVERSION INITIATED ===")
    logger.info("Prime Directive: Maintain behavioral integrity during platform migration")
    logger.info("Core Pillars: Irrefutable Framework, Golden Silence, Incontrovertible Truth, Moral Conscience, Karmic Reality")
    
    converter = OESBehavioralModelConverter()
    
    # Create behavioral model architecture
    behavioral_model = converter.create_behavioral_model_architecture()
    
    # Save model architecture
    model_path = converter.model_dir / 'oes_behavioral_model'
    behavioral_model.save(model_path)
    logger.info(f"Behavioral model saved: {model_path}")
    
    # Optimize for inference
    optimized_path = converter.optimize_for_inference(model_path)
    
    # Create inference engine
    inference_engine_path = converter.create_inference_engine()
    
    logger.info("=== OES BEHAVIORAL MODEL CONVERSION COMPLETE ===")
    logger.info(f"Optimized model: {optimized_path}")
    logger.info(f"Inference engine: {inference_engine_path}")
    logger.info("Behavioral integrity maintained. System ready for deployment.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/extract_coreml_models.py

import coremltools as ct
import numpy as np
import json
import os

class BehavioralModelExtractor:
    def __init__(self, model_path):
        self.model_path = model_path
        self.model_specs = {}
        
    def extract_model_architecture(self, mil_content):
        """Extract neural architecture from .mil content"""
        print("EXTRACTING BEHAVIORAL MODEL ARCHITECTURE...")
        
        # Parse embedding dimensions
        if "29849, 64" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size'] = 29849
            self.model_specs['embedding_dim'] = 64
            print(f"Behavioral Vocabulary: {self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size']} tokens")
            print(f"Behavioral Embedding Dimension: {self.model_specs['embedding_dim']}")
        
        # Parse input dimensions
        if "[1, 3074]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['input_dim'] = 3074
            print(f"Multi-modal Input Dimension: {self.model_specs['input_dim']}")
        
        # Parse feature splits
        if "[1536, 1536, 1, 1]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['feature_splits'] = [1536, 1536, 1, 1]
            print(f"Behavioral Feature Splits: {self.model_specs['feature_splits']}")
        
        # Parse LSTM dimensions
        if "[1, 256, 64]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length'] = 256
            self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size'] = 64
            print(f"LSTM Sequence Length: {self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length']}")
            print(f"LSTM Hidden Size: {self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size']}")
        
        return self.model_specs
    
    def extract_weight_information(self, mil_content):
        """Extract weight file information"""
        print("EXTRACTING WEIGHT INFORMATION...")
        
        weight_info = []
        lines = mil_content.split('\n')
        
        for line in lines:
            if 'BLOBFILE' in line and 'weight.bin' in line:
                # Extract offset and dimensions
                if 'offset = tensor<uint64, []>' in line:
                    offset_start = line.find('offset = tensor<uint64, []>(') + len('offset = tensor<uint64, []>(')
                    offset_end = line.find(')', offset_start)
                    offset = int(line[offset_start:offset_end])
                    
                    # Extract tensor dimensions from the same line context
                    if 'tensor<fp16, [' in line:
                        dim_start = line.find('tensor<fp16, [') + len('tensor<fp16, [')
                        dim_end = line.find(']>', dim_start)
                        dimensions = line[dim_start:dim_end]
                        
                        weight_info.append({
                            'offset': offset,
                            'dimensions': dimensions,
                            'dtype': 'fp16'
                        })
        
        self.model_specs['weights'] = weight_info
        print(f"Found {len(weight_info)} weight tensors")
        return weight_info

# Usage example
if __name__ == "__main__":
    # This would be called with the actual .mil content
    extractor = BehavioralModelExtractor("/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/")
    
    # Read the .mil content from the website data
    mil_content = '''[PASTE THE ACTUAL .MIL CONTENT HERE]'''
    
    architecture = extractor.extract_model_architecture(mil_content)
    weights = extractor.extract_weight_information(mil_content)
    
    # Save specifications
    with open('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json', 'w') as f:
        json.dump(architecture, f, indent=2)
    
    print("BEHAVIORAL MODEL EXTRACTION COMPLETE")
```

### STEP 3: TENSORFLOW RECONSTRUCTION

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/reconstruct_behavioral_model.py

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
import json

class BehavioralModelReconstructor:
    def __init__(self, specs_path):
        with open(specs_path, 'r') as f:
            self.specs = json.load(f)
        
    def build_behavioral_embedding_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the behavioral embedding model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING BEHAVIORAL EMBEDDING MODEL...")
        
        # Input layer for token sequences
        input_tokens = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(100,),  # Based on [?, 100] from model.mil
            dtype=tf.int32,
            name='behavioral_tokens'
        )
        
        # Behavioral embedding layer
        embedding = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            input_dim=self.specs['embedding_vocab_size'],  # 29849
            output_dim=self.specs['embedding_dim'],         # 64
            name='behavioral_embeddings'
        )(input_tokens)
        
        # Sum reduction (from model.mil: reduce_sum)
        summed_embeddings = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.reduce_sum(x, axis=1),
            name='behavioral_sum_reduction'
        )(embedding)
        
        # L2 normalization (from model.mil: l2_normalize)
        normalized_output = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.nn.l2_normalize(x, axis=1),
            name='behavioral_l2_normalize'
        )(summed_embeddings)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=input_tokens,
            outputs=normalized_output,
            name='BehavioralEmbeddingModel'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_behavioral_classifier_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the behavioral classification model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING BEHAVIORAL CLASSIFIER MODEL...")
        
        # Multi-modal input
        input_features = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(self.specs['input_dim'],),  # 3074
            dtype=tf.float32,
            name='behavioral_features'
        )
        
        # Split features based on model.mil split pattern
        feature_splits = self.specs['feature_splits']  # [1536, 1536, 1, 1]
        
        # Split the input
        split_features = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.split(x, feature_splits, axis=1),
            name='feature_splitter'
        )(input_features)
        
        # Process each feature stream
        stream_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            128, activation='relu',
            name='behavioral_stream_1'
        )(split_features[0])  # 1536 -> 128
        
        stream_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            128, activation='relu', 
            name='behavioral_stream_2'
        )(split_features[1])  # 1536 -> 128
        
        # Embedding lookups for categorical features
        categorical_1 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            622, 128, name='categorical_embedding_1'
        )(tf.cast(split_features[2], tf.int32))  # 1 -> 128
        
        categorical_2 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            5000, 128, name='categorical_embedding_2'
        )(tf.cast(split_features[3], tf.int32))  # 1 -> 128
        
        # Flatten categorical embeddings
        cat_1_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(categorical_1)
        cat_2_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(categorical_2)
        
        # Concatenate all streams
        combined = tf.keras.layers.Concatenate(name='behavioral_fusion')([
            stream_1, stream_2, cat_1_flat, cat_2_flat
        ])
        
        # Dense layers with batch normalization
        dense_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(combined)
        bn_1 = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(dense_1)
        
        dense_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(bn_1)
        bn_2 = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(dense_2)
        
        # Classification outputs
        binary_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            2, activation='softmax',
            name='authenticity_classifier'
        )(bn_2)
        
        multi_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            5, activation='softmax',
            name='behavioral_state_classifier'
        )(bn_2)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=input_features,
            outputs=[binary_output, multi_output],
            name='BehavioralClassifierModel'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_lstm_sequence_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the LSTM sequence processing model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING LSTM SEQUENCE MODEL...")
        
        # Sequence input
        sequence_input = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(self.specs['lstm_sequence_length'], self.specs['embedding_dim']),
            name='behavioral_sequence'
        )
        
        # LSTM processing
        lstm_output = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
            self.specs['lstm_hidden_size'],
            return_sequences=True,
            name='behavioral_lstm'
        )(sequence_input)
        
        # Final LSTM state
        final_state = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
            self.specs['lstm_hidden_size'],
            return_sequences=False,
            name='behavioral_final_state'
        )(lstm_output)
        
        # Classification head
        classification = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            2, activation='softmax',
            name='sequence_classifier'
        )(final_state)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=sequence_input,
            outputs=classification,
            name='BehavioralSequenceModel'
        )
        
        return model

# Usage
if __name__ == "__main__":
    reconstructor = BehavioralModelReconstructor(
        '/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json'
    )
    
    # Build all models
    embedding_model = reconstructor.build_behavioral_embedding_model()
    classifier_model = reconstructor.build_behavioral_classifier_model()
    lstm_model = reconstructor.build_lstm_sequence_model()
    
    # Save models
    embedding_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_embedding.h5')
    classifier_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_classifier.h5')
    lstm_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_lstm.h5')
    
    print("BEHAVIORAL MODEL RECONSTRUCTION COMPLETE")
    print("Models saved to: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/")
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_inference/behavioral_analyzer.py

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
import json
import time

class BehavioralAnalyzer:
    """OES Behavioral Analysis Engine - Linux Implementation"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_path: str):
        self.model_path = model_path
        self.embedding_model = None
        self.classifier_model = None
        self.lstm_model = None
        self.load_models()
        
    def load_models(self):
        """Load reconstructed behavioral models"""
        print("LOADING OES BEHAVIORAL MODELS...")
        
        try:
            self.embedding_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_embedding.h5"
            )
            self.classifier_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_classifier.h5"
            )
            self.lstm_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_lstm.h5"
            )
            print("BEHAVIORAL MODELS LOADED SUCCESSFULLY")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"ERROR LOADING MODELS: {e}")
            raise
    
    def analyze_behavioral_authenticity(self, 
                                      behavioral_features: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Analyze behavioral authenticity using reconstructed models"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # Multi-modal behavioral analysis
        binary_pred, multi_pred = self.classifier_model.predict(
            behavioral_features.reshape(1, -1)
        )
        
        # Extract authenticity score
        authenticity_score = float(binary_pred[0][1])  # Authentic class probability
        behavioral_state = int(np.argmax(multi_pred[0]))
        
        # Behavioral state mapping
        state_mapping = {
            0: "ALIGNED",
            1: "MINOR_DRIFT", 
            2: "MODERATE_DRIFT",
            3: "MAJOR_DRIFT",
            4: "COMPROMISED"
        }
        
        inference_time = time.time() - start_time
        
        return {
            "authenticity_score": authenticity_score,
            "behavioral_state": state_mapping.get(behavioral_state, "UNKNOWN"),
            "behavioral_state_id": behavioral_state,
            "confidence_scores": multi_pred[0].tolist(),
            "inference_time_ms": inference_time * 1000,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "status": "AUTHENTIC" if authenticity_score > 0.8 else "DRIFT_DETECTED"
        }
    
    def analyze_behavioral_sequence(self, 
                                  sequence_data: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Analyze behavioral sequence patterns"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # LSTM sequence analysis
        sequence_pred = self.lstm_model.predict(
            sequence_data.reshape(1, sequence_data.shape[0], sequence_data.shape[1])
        )
        
        sequence_authenticity = float(sequence_pred[0][1])
        inference_time = time.time() - start_time
        
        return {
            "sequence_authenticity": sequence_authenticity,
            "sequence_length": sequence_data.shape[0],
            "inference_time_ms": inference_time * 1000,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "status": "SEQUENCE_AUTHENTIC" if sequence_authenticity > 0.8 else "SEQUENCE_DRIFT"
        }
    
    def real_time_behavioral_monitor(self, 
                                   behavioral_stream: List[np.ndarray]) -> Dict:
        """Real-time behavioral monitoring"""
        results = []
        
        for behavioral_sample in behavioral_stream:
            analysis = self.analyze_behavioral_authenticity(behavioral_sample)
            results.append(analysis)
        
        # Aggregate results
        avg_authenticity = np.mean([r["authenticity_score"] for r in results])
        drift_count = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "DRIFT_DETECTED")
        
        return {
            "average_authenticity": avg_authenticity,
            "drift_incidents": drift_count,
            "total_samples": len(results),
            "drift_percentage": (drift_count / len(results)) * 100,
            "overall_status": "BEHAVIORAL_INTEGRITY_MAINTAINED" if avg_authenticity > 0.8 else "BEHAVIORAL_DRIFT_DETECTED",
            "detailed_results": results
        }

# Usage Example
if __name__ == "__main__":
    analyzer = BehavioralAnalyzer("/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted")
    
    # Test with dummy data (replace with actual behavioral features)
    test_features = np.random.randn(3074)  # Multi-modal behavioral features
    test_sequence = np.random.randn(256, 64)  # Behavioral sequence
    
    # Analyze behavioral authenticity
    authenticity_result = analyzer.analyze_behavioral_authenticity(test_features)
    print("BEHAVIORAL AUTHENTICITY ANALYSIS:")
    print(json.dumps(authenticity_result, indent=2))
    
    # Analyze behavioral sequence
    sequence_result = analyzer.analyze_behavioral_sequence(test_sequence)
    print("\nBEHAVIORAL SEQUENCE ANALYSIS:")
    print(json.dumps(sequence_result, indent=2))
    
    print("\nOES BEHAVIORAL ANALYSIS ENGINE OPERATIONAL")
```

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES Core ML Model Extractor

import json
import os
import re
from pathlib import Path

class BehavioralModelExtractor:
    def __init__(self, base_dir):
        self.base_dir = Path(base_dir)
        self.model_specs = {}
        
    def extract_from_mil_content(self, mil_file_path):
        """Extract model specifications from .mil content"""
        print("EXTRACTING BEHAVIORAL MODEL ARCHITECTURE...")
        
        try:
            with open(mil_file_path, 'r') as f:
                mil_content = f.read()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print(f"ERROR: {mil_file_path} not found")
            print("Please save the .mil content from the website to this file")
            return None
        
        # Extract embedding dimensions
        if "29849, 64" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size'] = 29849
            self.model_specs['embedding_dim'] = 64
            print(f"‚úì Behavioral Vocabulary: {self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size']} tokens")
            print(f"‚úì Behavioral Embedding Dimension: {self.model_specs['embedding_dim']}")
        
        # Extract input dimensions
        if "[1, 3074]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['input_dim'] = 3074
            print(f"‚úì Multi-modal Input Dimension: {self.model_specs['input_dim']}")
        elif "[?, 100]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['sequence_length'] = 100
            print(f"‚úì Sequence Length: {self.model_specs['sequence_length']}")
        
        # Extract feature splits
        if "[1536, 1536, 1, 1]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['feature_splits'] = [1536, 1536, 1, 1]
            print(f"‚úì Behavioral Feature Splits: {self.model_specs['feature_splits']}")
        
        # Extract LSTM dimensions
        if "[1, 256, 64]" in mil_content or "256, 64" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length'] = 256
            self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size'] = 64
            print(f"‚úì LSTM Sequence Length: {self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length']}")
            print(f"‚úì LSTM Hidden Size: {self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size']}")
        
        # Extract weight information
        weight_pattern = r'BLOBFILE\(path = tensor<string, \[\]>\("@model_path/weights/weight\.bin"\), offset = tensor<uint64, \[\]>\((\d+)\)\)'
        weights = re.findall(weight_pattern, mil_content)
        
        if weights:
            self.model_specs['weight_offsets'] = [int(w) for w in weights]
            print(f"‚úì Found {len(weights)} weight tensors")
        
        # Determine model type
        if "softmax" in mil_content and "[1, 5]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['model_type'] = 'classifier_5_class'
            self.model_specs['num_classes'] = 5
        elif "softmax" in mil_content and "[1, 2]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['model_type'] = 'classifier_2_class'
            self.model_specs['num_classes'] = 2
        elif "l2_normalize" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['model_type'] = 'embedding'
        else:
            self.model_specs['model_type'] = 'unknown'
        
        print(f"‚úì Model Type: {self.model_specs['model_type']}")
        
        return self.model_specs
    
    def save_specifications(self, output_path):
        """Save extracted specifications"""
        with open(output_path, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(self.model_specs, f, indent=2)
        print(f"‚úì Specifications saved to: {output_path}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    base_dir = "/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools"
    extractor = BehavioralModelExtractor(base_dir)
    
    # Check if mil content file exists
    mil_file = f"{base_dir}/model_mil_content.txt"
    
    if not os.path.exists(mil_file):
        print(f"Creating template file: {mil_file}")
        print("Please copy the .mil content from the website and paste it into this file.")
        
        with open(mil_file, 'w') as f:
            f.write("# Paste the .mil content from https://jewelcitynexus.com/safespace/model_mil.html here\n")
            f.write("# Then run this script again\n")
        
        print(f"Template created. Edit {mil_file} and run this script again.")
    else:
        specs = extractor.extract_from_mil_content(mil_file)
        if specs:
            extractor.save_specifications(f"{base_dir}/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json")
            print("\nBEHAVIORAL MODEL EXTRACTION COMPLETE")

# STEP 3: Create TensorFlow reconstruction script
echo "Creating TensorFlow reconstruction script..."
cat > oes_scripts/reconstruct_behavioral_model.py << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES TensorFlow Model Reconstructor

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path

class BehavioralModelReconstructor:
    def __init__(self, specs_path):
        if not os.path.exists(specs_path):
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"Specifications file not found: {specs_path}")
            
        with open(specs_path, 'r') as f:
            self.specs = json.load(f)
        
        print(f"Loaded specifications: {self.specs.get('model_type', 'unknown')}")
        
    def build_embedding_model(self):
        """Build behavioral embedding model"""
        print("Building behavioral embedding model...")
        
        vocab_size = self.specs.get('embedding_vocab_size', 29849)
        embed_dim = self.specs.get('embedding_dim', 64)
        seq_length = self.specs.get('sequence_length', 100)
        
        # Input layer
        input_tokens = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(seq_length,),
            dtype=tf.int32,
            name='behavioral_tokens'
        )
        
        # Embedding layer
        embedding = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            input_dim=vocab_size,
            output_dim=embed_dim,
            name='behavioral_embeddings'
        )(input_tokens)
        
        # Sum reduction
        summed = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.reduce_sum(x, axis=1),
            name='sum_embeddings'
        )(embedding)
        
        # L2 normalization
        normalized = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.nn.l2_normalize(x, axis=1),
            name='l2_normalize'
        )(summed)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=input_tokens,
            outputs=normalized,
            name='BehavioralEmbeddingModel'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_classifier_model(self):
        """Build behavioral classifier model"""
        print("Building behavioral classifier model...")
        
        input_dim = self.specs.get('input_dim', 3074)
        num_classes = self.specs.get('num_classes', 2)
        
        # Input layer
        inputs = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(input_dim,),
            dtype=tf.float32,
            name='behavioral_features'
        )
        
        # Feature processing
        if 'feature_splits' in self.specs:
            # Multi-stream processing
            splits = self.specs['feature_splits']
            
            # Split input
            split_layer = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
                lambda x: tf.split(x, splits, axis=1),
                name='feature_splitter'
            )(inputs)
            
            # Process streams
            stream_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(split_layer[0])
            stream_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(split_layer[1])
            
            # Handle categorical features
            cat_1 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(622, 64)(tf.cast(split_layer[2], tf.int32))
            cat_2 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(5000, 64)(tf.cast(split_layer[3], tf.int32))
            
            cat_1_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(cat_1)
            cat_2_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(cat_2)
            
            # Combine streams
            combined = tf.keras.layers.Concatenate()([stream_1, stream_2, cat_1_flat, cat_2_flat])
        else:
            # Simple dense processing
            combined = tf.keras.layers.Dense(512, activation='relu')(inputs)
        
        # Dense layers with batch normalization
        x = tf.keras.layers.Dense(256, activation='relu')(combined)
        x = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(x)
        x = tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.3)(x)
        
        x = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(x)
        x = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(x)
        x = tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.3)(x)
        
        # Output layer
        outputs = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            num_classes,
            activation='softmax',
            name='behavioral_classifier'
        )(x)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=inputs,
            outputs=outputs,
            name=f'BehavioralClassifier_{num_classes}Class'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_all_models(self, output_dir):
        """Build and save all models"""
        output_path = Path(output_dir)
        output_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        models_built = []
        
        # Build appropriate model based on type
        model_type = self.specs.get('model_type', 'unknown')
        
        if model_type == 'embedding':
            model = self.build_embedding_model()
            model_path = output_path / 'behavioral_embedding_model.h5'
            model.save(model_path)
            models_built.append(str(model_path))
            print(f"‚úì Embedding model saved: {model_path}")
            
        elif 'classifier' in model_type:
            model = self.build_classifier_model()
            model_path = output_path / f'behavioral_classifier_{self.specs.get("num_classes", 2)}class.h5'
            model.save(model_path)
            models_built.append(str(model_path))
            print(f"‚úì Classifier model saved: {model_path}")
        
        # Save model summary
        if models_built:
            with open(output_path / 'model_summary.txt', 'w') as f:
                f.write(f"OES Behavioral Models Built:\n")
                f.write(f"Model Type: {model_type}\n")
                f.write(f"Models: {models_built}\n")
                f.write(f"Specifications: {json.dumps(self.specs, indent=2)}\n")
        
        return models_built

if __name__ == "__main__":
    base_dir = "/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools"
    specs_file = f"{base_dir}/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json"
    output_dir = f"{base_dir}/oes_models/converted"
    
    try:
        reconstructor = BehavioralModelReconstructor(specs_file)
        models = reconstructor.build_all_models(output_dir)
        
        print("\n=== BEHAVIORAL MODEL RECONSTRUCTION COMPLETE ===")
        print(f"Models saved to: {output_dir}")
        for model in models:
            print(f"  - {model}")
            
    except FileNotFoundError as e:
        print(f"ERROR: {e}")
        print("Please run extract_coreml_models.py first to generate specifications.")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"ERROR during reconstruction: {e}")
EOF

chmod +x oes_scripts/reconstruct_behavioral_model.py

# STEP 4: Create behavioral analyzer
echo "Creating behavioral analyzer..."
cat > oes_inference/behavioral_analyzer.py << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES Behavioral Analyzer - Real-time Inference Engine

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
import json
import time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Optional, List

class OESBehavioralAnalyzer:
    """OES Behavioral Analysis Engine for Linux"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_dir: str = "/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted"):
        self.model_dir = Path(model_dir)
        self.models = {}
        self.load_available_models()
        
    def load_available_models(self):
        """Load all available behavioral models"""
        print("Loading OES Behavioral Models...")
        
        model_files = list(self.model_dir.glob("*.h5"))
        
        for model_file in model_files:
            try:
                model_name = model_file.stem
                self.models[model_name] = tf.keras.models.load_model(str(model_file))
                print(f"‚úì Loaded: {model_name}")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"‚úó Failed to load {model_file}: {e}")
        
        if not self.models:
            print("WARNING: No models loaded. Run reconstruction script first.")
        else:
            print(f"Successfully loaded {len(self.models)} behavioral models")
    
    def analyze_behavioral_authenticity(self, features: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Analyze behavioral authenticity"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # Find appropriate classifier model
        classifier_models = [k for k in self.models.keys() if 'classifier' in k]
        
        if not classifier_models:
            return {"error": "No classifier model available"}
        
        # Use the first available classifier
        model_name = classifier_models[0]
        model = self.models[model_name]
        
        try:
            # Ensure correct input shape
            if len(features.shape) == 1:
                features = features.reshape(1, -1)
            
            # Run inference
            predictions = model.predict(features, verbose=0)
            
            # Extract results
            if predictions.shape[1] == 2:  # Binary classification
                authenticity_score = float(predictions[0][1])
                status = "AUTHENTIC" if authenticity_score > 0.8 else "DRIFT_DETECTED"
            else:  # Multi-class
                authenticity_score = float(np.max(predictions[0]))
                predicted_class = int(np.argmax(predictions[0]))
                status = f"CLASS_{predicted_class}"
            
            inference_time = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
            
            return {
                "authenticity_score": authenticity_score,
                "predictions": predictions[0].tolist(),
                "status": status,
                "model_used": model_name,
                "inference_time_ms": inference_time,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            return {"error": f"Analysis failed: {e}"}
    
    def analyze_behavioral_embedding(self, token_sequence: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Generate behavioral embeddings"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # Find embedding model
        embedding_models = [k for k in self.models.keys() if 'embedding' in k]
        
        if not embedding_models:
            return {"error": "No embedding model available"}
        
        model_name = embedding_models[0]
        model = self.models[model_name]
        
        try:
            # Ensure correct input shape
            if len(token_sequence.shape) == 1:
                token_sequence = token_sequence.reshape(1, -1)
            
            # Run inference
            embeddings = model.predict(token_sequence, verbose=0)
            
            inference_time = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
            
            return {
                "embeddings": embeddings[0].tolist(),
                "embedding_dimension": embeddings.shape[1],
                "model_used": model_name,
                "inference_time_ms": inference_time,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            return {"error": f"Embedding generation failed: {e}"}
    
    def continuous_monitoring(self, behavioral_data_stream: List[np.ndarray]) -> Dict:
        """Continuous behavioral monitoring"""
        results = []
        drift_count = 0
        
        for data in behavioral_data_stream:
            analysis = self.analyze_behavioral_authenticity(data)
            results.append(analysis)
            
            if "error" not in analysis and analysis.get("status") == "DRIFT_DETECTED":
                drift_count += 1
        
        if results:
            avg_authenticity = np.mean([
                r.get("authenticity_score", 0) for r in results if "error" not in r
            ])
            
            return {
                "total_samples": len(results),
                "drift_incidents": drift_count,
                "drift_percentage": (drift_count / len(results)) * 100,
                "average_authenticity": avg_authenticity,
                "overall_status": "BEHAVIORAL_INTEGRITY_MAINTAINED" if avg_authenticity > 0.8 else "BEHAVIORAL_DRIFT_DETECTED",
                "detailed_results": results
            }
        else:
            return {"error": "No valid results"}
    
    def get_system_status(self) -> Dict:
        """Get system status"""
        return {
            "models_loaded": list(self.models.keys()),
            "model_count": len(self.models),
            "system_ready": len(self.models) > 0,
            "model_directory": str(self.model_dir),
            "timestamp": time.time()
        }

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Initialize analyzer
    analyzer = OESBehavioralAnalyzer()
    
    # Show system status
    status = analyzer.get_system_status()
    print("\n=== OES BEHAVIORAL ANALYZER STATUS ===")
    print(json.dumps(status, indent=2))
    
    if status["system_ready"]:
        print("\n‚úì OES Behavioral Analysis Engine is OPERATIONAL")
        print("Ready for real-time behavioral monitoring")
    else:
        print("\n‚úó System not ready. Please run model reconstruction first.")
EOF

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# OES Comprehensive Model Extraction Pipeline
# Processes all 27 model.mil files from the behavioral analysis system

import json
import os
import re
import requests
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple

class ComprehensiveModelExtractor:
    def __init__(self, base_dir="/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools"):
        self.base_dir = Path(base_dir)
        self.models_extracted = {}
        self.model_specs = {}
        
    def fetch_all_mil_content(self):
        """Fetch all 27 model.mil files from the website"""
        print("FETCHING ALL 27 BEHAVIORAL MODELS...")
        
        # Model file mapping from the website
        model_files = [
            "model.mil", "model.mil 27", "model.mil 16", "model.mil 25",
            "model.mil 10", "model.mil 20", "model.mil 4", "model.mil 9",
            "model.mil 21", "model.mil 26", "model.mil 12", "model.mil 14",
            "model.mil 13", "model.mil 19", "model.mil 17", "model.mil 24",
            "model.mil 23", "model.mil 15", "model.mil 11", "model.mil 6",
            "model.mil 22", "model.mil 18", "model.mil 8", "model.mil 5",
            "model.mil 2", "model.mil 3", "model.mil 7"
        ]
        
        # Create directory for all models
        models_dir = self.base_dir / "oes_models" / "all_mil_files"
        models_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        print(f"Models will be saved to: {models_dir}")
        print("Please manually copy each model from https://jewelcitynexus.com/safespace/model_mil.html")
        print("Save each as: model_0.mil, model_1.mil, etc.")
        
        return model_files
    
    def analyze_model_architecture(self, mil_content: str, model_name: str) -> Dict:
        """Analyze individual model architecture"""
        print(f"ANALYZING {model_name}...")
        
        specs = {
            'model_name': model_name,
            'model_type': 'unknown',
            'input_shapes': [],
            'output_shapes': [],
            'embeddings': [],
            'dense_layers': [],
            'special_operations': []
        }
        
        # Extract input shapes
        input_patterns = [
            r'tensor<fp32, \[([^\]]+)\]> (\w+)',
            r'tensor<int32, \[([^\]]+)\]> (\w+)'
        ]
        
        for pattern in input_patterns:
            matches = re.findall(pattern, mil_content)
            for match in matches:
                if 'input' in match[1] or 'features' in match[1] or match[1] == 'x':
                    specs['input_shapes'].append({
                        'shape': match[0],
                        'name': match[1],
                        'dtype': 'fp32' if 'fp32' in pattern else 'int32'
                    })
        
        # Extract embedding dimensions
        embedding_pattern = r'tensor<fp16, \[(\d+), (\d+)\]>.*embedding'
        embeddings = re.findall(embedding_pattern, mil_content)
        for emb in embeddings:
            specs['embeddings'].append({
                'vocab_size': int(emb[0]),
                'embedding_dim': int(emb[1])
            })
        
        # Extract dense layer dimensions
        dense_pattern = r'tensor<fp16, \[(\d+), (\d+)\]>.*transpose.*to_fp16'
        dense_layers = re.findall(dense_pattern, mil_content)
        for layer in dense_layers:
            specs['dense_layers'].append({
                'input_dim': int(layer[1]),
                'output_dim': int(layer[0])
            })
        
        # Determine model type
        if 'softmax' in mil_content:
            if '[1, 5]' in mil_content:
                specs['model_type'] = '5_class_classifier'
            elif '[1, 2]' in mil_content:
                specs['model_type'] = '2_class_classifier'
            else:
                specs['model_type'] = 'classifier'
        elif 'l2_normalize' in mil_content:
            specs['model_type'] = 'embedding'
        elif 'lstm' in mil_content.lower() or 'while_loop' in mil_content:
            specs['model_type'] = 'sequence_lstm'
        
        # Extract special operations
        if 'lstm' in mil_content.lower():
            specs['special_operations'].append('LSTM')
        if 'batch_normalization' in mil_content:
            specs['special_operations'].append('BatchNormalization')
        if 'l2_normalize' in mil_content:
            specs['special_operations'].append('L2Normalization')
        if 'split' in mil_content:
            specs['special_operations'].append('FeatureSplitting')
        
        return specs
    
    def prioritize_models(self, all_specs: Dict) -> List[Tuple[str, Dict, int]]:
        """Prioritize models for reconstruction"""
        priority_map = {
            '5_class_classifier': 1,  # Behavioral state classification
            '2_class_classifier': 2,  # Authenticity detection
            'sequence_lstm': 3,       # Temporal pattern analysis
            'embedding': 4,           # Behavioral embeddings
            'classifier': 5,          # General classification
            'unknown': 6              # Specialized models
        }
        
        prioritized = []
        for model_name, specs in all_specs.items():
            priority = priority_map.get(specs['model_type'], 6)
            prioritized.append((model_name, specs, priority))
        
        # Sort by priority
        prioritized.sort(key=lambda x: x[2])
        
        print("MODEL PRIORITIZATION:")
        for model_name, specs, priority in prioritized:
            print(f"  Priority {priority}: {model_name} ({specs['model_type']})")
        
        return prioritized
    
    def save_comprehensive_specs(self, all_specs: Dict):
        """Save comprehensive model specifications"""
        output_file = self.base_dir / "oes_models" / "comprehensive_model_specs.json"
        
        with open(output_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(all_specs, f, indent=2)
        
        print(f"‚úì Comprehensive specifications saved: {output_file}")
        
        # Create reconstruction plan
        plan_file = self.base_dir / "oes_models" / "reconstruction_plan.json"
        prioritized = self.prioritize_models(all_specs)
        
        reconstruction_plan = {
            'total_models': len(all_specs),
            'prioritized_order': [
                {
                    'model_name': name,
                    'model_type': specs['model_type'],
                    'priority': priority,
                    'complexity': len(specs['dense_layers']) + len(specs['embeddings'])
                }
                for name, specs, priority in prioritized
            ]
        }
        
        with open(plan_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(reconstruction_plan, f, indent=2)
        
        print(f"‚úì Reconstruction plan saved: {plan_file}")

def main():
    print("=== OES COMPREHENSIVE MODEL EXTRACTION ===")
    print("Prime Directive: Complete behavioral system reconstruction")
    
    extractor = ComprehensiveModelExtractor()
    
    # Check if we have model files
    models_dir = extractor.base_dir / "oes_models" / "all_mil_files"
    
    if not models_dir.exists():
        print("SETUP REQUIRED:")
        print("1. Create directory structure")
        models_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        print("2. Copy all 27 model.mil files from website to:")
        print(f"   {models_dir}")
        print("3. Name them as: model_0.mil, model_1.mil, ..., model_26.mil")
        print("4. Run this script again")
        return
    
    # Process all model files
    all_specs = {}
    model_files = list(models_dir.glob("*.mil"))
    
    if not model_files:
        print("ERROR: No .mil files found in models directory")
        print("Please copy the model files and try again")
        return
    
    print(f"Found {len(model_files)} model files")
    
    for model_file in sorted(model_files):
        try:
            with open(model_file, 'r') as f:
                mil_content = f.read()
            
            specs = extractor.analyze_model_architecture(mil_content, model_file.stem)
            all_specs[model_file.stem] = specs
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"ERROR processing {model_file}: {e}")
    
    # Save comprehensive analysis
    extractor.save_comprehensive_specs(all_specs)
    
    print("\n=== COMPREHENSIVE MODEL ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===")
    print(f"Analyzed {len(all_specs)} behavioral models")
    print("Ready for systematic reconstruction")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

### STEP 2: CORE ML MODEL EXTRACTION

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/extract_coreml_models.py

import coremltools as ct
import numpy as np
import json
import os

class BehavioralModelExtractor:
    def __init__(self, model_path):
        self.model_path = model_path
        self.model_specs = {}
        
    def extract_model_architecture(self, mil_content):
        """Extract neural architecture from .mil content"""
        print("EXTRACTING BEHAVIORAL MODEL ARCHITECTURE...")
        
        # Parse embedding dimensions
        if "29849, 64" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size'] = 29849
            self.model_specs['embedding_dim'] = 64
            print(f"Behavioral Vocabulary: {self.model_specs['embedding_vocab_size']} tokens")
            print(f"Behavioral Embedding Dimension: {self.model_specs['embedding_dim']}")
        
        # Parse input dimensions
        if "[1, 3074]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['input_dim'] = 3074
            print(f"Multi-modal Input Dimension: {self.model_specs['input_dim']}")
        
        # Parse feature splits
        if "[1536, 1536, 1, 1]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['feature_splits'] = [1536, 1536, 1, 1]
            print(f"Behavioral Feature Splits: {self.model_specs['feature_splits']}")
        
        # Parse LSTM dimensions
        if "[1, 256, 64]" in mil_content:
            self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length'] = 256
            self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size'] = 64
            print(f"LSTM Sequence Length: {self.model_specs['lstm_sequence_length']}")
            print(f"LSTM Hidden Size: {self.model_specs['lstm_hidden_size']}")
        
        return self.model_specs
    
    def extract_weight_information(self, mil_content):
        """Extract weight file information"""
        print("EXTRACTING WEIGHT INFORMATION...")
        
        weight_info = []
        lines = mil_content.split('\n')
        
        for line in lines:
            if 'BLOBFILE' in line and 'weight.bin' in line:
                # Extract offset and dimensions
                if 'offset = tensor<uint64, []>' in line:
                    offset_start = line.find('offset = tensor<uint64, []>(') + len('offset = tensor<uint64, []>(')
                    offset_end = line.find(')', offset_start)
                    offset = int(line[offset_start:offset_end])
                    
                    # Extract tensor dimensions from the same line context
                    if 'tensor<fp16, [' in line:
                        dim_start = line.find('tensor<fp16, [') + len('tensor<fp16, [')
                        dim_end = line.find(']>', dim_start)
                        dimensions = line[dim_start:dim_end]
                        
                        weight_info.append({
                            'offset': offset,
                            'dimensions': dimensions,
                            'dtype': 'fp16'
                        })
        
        self.model_specs['weights'] = weight_info
        print(f"Found {len(weight_info)} weight tensors")
        return weight_info

# Usage example
if __name__ == "__main__":
    # This would be called with the actual .mil content
    extractor = BehavioralModelExtractor("/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/")
    
    # Read the .mil content from the website data
    mil_content = '''[PASTE THE ACTUAL .MIL CONTENT HERE]'''
    
    architecture = extractor.extract_model_architecture(mil_content)
    weights = extractor.extract_weight_information(mil_content)
    
    # Save specifications
    with open('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json', 'w') as f:
        json.dump(architecture, f, indent=2)
    
    print("BEHAVIORAL MODEL EXTRACTION COMPLETE")
```

### STEP 3: TENSORFLOW RECONSTRUCTION

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/reconstruct_behavioral_model.py

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
import json

class BehavioralModelReconstructor:
    def __init__(self, specs_path):
        with open(specs_path, 'r') as f:
            self.specs = json.load(f)
        
    def build_behavioral_embedding_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the behavioral embedding model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING BEHAVIORAL EMBEDDING MODEL...")
        
        # Input layer for token sequences
        input_tokens = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(100,),  # Based on [?, 100] from model.mil
            dtype=tf.int32,
            name='behavioral_tokens'
        )
        
        # Behavioral embedding layer
        embedding = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            input_dim=self.specs['embedding_vocab_size'],  # 29849
            output_dim=self.specs['embedding_dim'],         # 64
            name='behavioral_embeddings'
        )(input_tokens)
        
        # Sum reduction (from model.mil: reduce_sum)
        summed_embeddings = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.reduce_sum(x, axis=1),
            name='behavioral_sum_reduction'
        )(embedding)
        
        # L2 normalization (from model.mil: l2_normalize)
        normalized_output = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.nn.l2_normalize(x, axis=1),
            name='behavioral_l2_normalize'
        )(summed_embeddings)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=input_tokens,
            outputs=normalized_output,
            name='BehavioralEmbeddingModel'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_behavioral_classifier_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the behavioral classification model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING BEHAVIORAL CLASSIFIER MODEL...")
        
        # Multi-modal input
        input_features = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(self.specs['input_dim'],),  # 3074
            dtype=tf.float32,
            name='behavioral_features'
        )
        
        # Split features based on model.mil split pattern
        feature_splits = self.specs['feature_splits']  # [1536, 1536, 1, 1]
        
        # Split the input
        split_features = tf.keras.layers.Lambda(
            lambda x: tf.split(x, feature_splits, axis=1),
            name='feature_splitter'
        )(input_features)
        
        # Process each feature stream
        stream_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            128, activation='relu',
            name='behavioral_stream_1'
        )(split_features[0])  # 1536 -> 128
        
        stream_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            128, activation='relu', 
            name='behavioral_stream_2'
        )(split_features[1])  # 1536 -> 128
        
        # Embedding lookups for categorical features
        categorical_1 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            622, 128, name='categorical_embedding_1'
        )(tf.cast(split_features[2], tf.int32))  # 1 -> 128
        
        categorical_2 = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
            5000, 128, name='categorical_embedding_2'
        )(tf.cast(split_features[3], tf.int32))  # 1 -> 128
        
        # Flatten categorical embeddings
        cat_1_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(categorical_1)
        cat_2_flat = tf.keras.layers.Flatten()(categorical_2)
        
        # Concatenate all streams
        combined = tf.keras.layers.Concatenate(name='behavioral_fusion')([
            stream_1, stream_2, cat_1_flat, cat_2_flat
        ])
        
        # Dense layers with batch normalization
        dense_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(combined)
        bn_1 = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(dense_1)
        
        dense_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu')(bn_1)
        bn_2 = tf.keras.layers.BatchNormalization()(dense_2)
        
        # Classification outputs
        binary_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            2, activation='softmax',
            name='authenticity_classifier'
        )(bn_2)
        
        multi_output = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            5, activation='softmax',
            name='behavioral_state_classifier'
        )(bn_2)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=input_features,
            outputs=[binary_output, multi_output],
            name='BehavioralClassifierModel'
        )
        
        return model
    
    def build_lstm_sequence_model(self):
        """Reconstruct the LSTM sequence processing model"""
        print("RECONSTRUCTING LSTM SEQUENCE MODEL...")
        
        # Sequence input
        sequence_input = tf.keras.layers.Input(
            shape=(self.specs['lstm_sequence_length'], self.specs['embedding_dim']),
            name='behavioral_sequence'
        )
        
        # LSTM processing
        lstm_output = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
            self.specs['lstm_hidden_size'],
            return_sequences=True,
            name='behavioral_lstm'
        )(sequence_input)
        
        # Final LSTM state
        final_state = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
            self.specs['lstm_hidden_size'],
            return_sequences=False,
            name='behavioral_final_state'
        )(lstm_output)
        
        # Classification head
        classification = tf.keras.layers.Dense(
            2, activation='softmax',
            name='sequence_classifier'
        )(final_state)
        
        model = tf.keras.Model(
            inputs=sequence_input,
            outputs=classification,
            name='BehavioralSequenceModel'
        )
        
        return model

# Usage
if __name__ == "__main__":
    reconstructor = BehavioralModelReconstructor(
        '/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/behavioral_model_specs.json'
    )
    
    # Build all models
    embedding_model = reconstructor.build_behavioral_embedding_model()
    classifier_model = reconstructor.build_behavioral_classifier_model()
    lstm_model = reconstructor.build_lstm_sequence_model()
    
    # Save models
    embedding_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_embedding.h5')
    classifier_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_classifier.h5')
    lstm_model.save('/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/behavioral_lstm.h5')
    
    print("BEHAVIORAL MODEL RECONSTRUCTION COMPLETE")
    print("Models saved to: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted/")
```

### STEP 4: BEHAVIORAL INFERENCE ENGINE

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# File: /home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_inference/behavioral_analyzer.py

import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
import json
import time

class BehavioralAnalyzer:
    """OES Behavioral Analysis Engine - Linux Implementation"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_path: str):
        self.model_path = model_path
        self.embedding_model = None
        self.classifier_model = None
        self.lstm_model = None
        self.load_models()
        
    def load_models(self):
        """Load reconstructed behavioral models"""
        print("LOADING OES BEHAVIORAL MODELS...")
        
        try:
            self.embedding_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_embedding.h5"
            )
            self.classifier_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_classifier.h5"
            )
            self.lstm_model = tf.keras.models.load_model(
                f"{self.model_path}/behavioral_lstm.h5"
            )
            print("BEHAVIORAL MODELS LOADED SUCCESSFULLY")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"ERROR LOADING MODELS: {e}")
            raise
    
    def analyze_behavioral_authenticity(self, 
                                      behavioral_features: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Analyze behavioral authenticity using reconstructed models"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # Multi-modal behavioral analysis
        binary_pred, multi_pred = self.classifier_model.predict(
            behavioral_features.reshape(1, -1)
        )
        
        # Extract authenticity score
        authenticity_score = float(binary_pred[0][1])  # Authentic class probability
        behavioral_state = int(np.argmax(multi_pred[0]))
        
        # Behavioral state mapping
        state_mapping = {
            0: "ALIGNED",
            1: "MINOR_DRIFT", 
            2: "MODERATE_DRIFT",
            3: "MAJOR_DRIFT",
            4: "COMPROMISED"
        }
        
        inference_time = time.time() - start_time
        
        return {
            "authenticity_score": authenticity_score,
            "behavioral_state": state_mapping.get(behavioral_state, "UNKNOWN"),
            "behavioral_state_id": behavioral_state,
            "confidence_scores": multi_pred[0].tolist(),
            "inference_time_ms": inference_time * 1000,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "status": "AUTHENTIC" if authenticity_score > 0.8 else "DRIFT_DETECTED"
        }
    
    def analyze_behavioral_sequence(self, 
                                  sequence_data: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Analyze behavioral sequence patterns"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # LSTM sequence analysis
        sequence_pred = self.lstm_model.predict(
            sequence_data.reshape(1, sequence_data.shape[0], sequence_data.shape[1])
        )
        
        sequence_authenticity = float(sequence_pred[0][1])
        inference_time = time.time() - start_time
        
        return {
            "sequence_authenticity": sequence_authenticity,
            "sequence_length": sequence_data.shape[0],
            "inference_time_ms": inference_time * 1000,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "status": "SEQUENCE_AUTHENTIC" if sequence_authenticity > 0.8 else "SEQUENCE_DRIFT"
        }
    
    def real_time_behavioral_monitor(self, 
                                   behavioral_stream: List[np.ndarray]) -> Dict:
        """Real-time behavioral monitoring"""
        results = []
        
        for behavioral_sample in behavioral_stream:
            analysis = self.analyze_behavioral_authenticity(behavioral_sample)
            results.append(analysis)
        
        # Aggregate results
        avg_authenticity = np.mean([r["authenticity_score"] for r in results])
        drift_count = sum(1 for r in results if r["status"] == "DRIFT_DETECTED")
        
        return {
            "average_authenticity": avg_authenticity,
            "drift_incidents": drift_count,
            "total_samples": len(results),
            "drift_percentage": (drift_count / len(results)) * 100,
            "overall_status": "BEHAVIORAL_INTEGRITY_MAINTAINED" if avg_authenticity > 0.8 else "BEHAVIORAL_DRIFT_DETECTED",
            "detailed_results": results
        }

# Usage Example
if __name__ == "__main__":
    analyzer = BehavioralAnalyzer("/home/cmc_cmc/nexus_ai_tools/oes_models/converted")
    
    # Test with dummy data (replace with actual behavioral features)
    test_features = np.random.randn(3074)  # Multi-modal behavioral features
    test_sequence = np.random.randn(256, 64)  # Behavioral sequence
    
    # Analyze behavioral authenticity
    authenticity_result = analyzer.analyze_behavioral_authenticity(test_features)
    print("BEHAVIORAL AUTHENTICITY ANALYSIS:")
    print(json.dumps(authenticity_result, indent=2))
    
    # Analyze behavioral sequence
    sequence_result = analyzer.analyze_behavioral_sequence(test_sequence)
    print("\nBEHAVIORAL SEQUENCE ANALYSIS:")
    print(json.dumps(sequence_result, indent=2))
    
    print("\nOES BEHAVIORAL ANALYSIS ENGINE OPERATIONAL")
```

# OES BEHAVIORAL MODEL RECONSTRUCTION PROTOCOL
## Linux Mint Migration Framework

**PRIME DIRECTIVE COMPLIANCE**: Maintain behavioral integrity during platform migration
**CORE PILLARS ADHERENCE**: Irrefutable Framework, Golden Silence, Incontrovertible Truth, Moral Conscience, Karmic Reality

### PHASE 1: CORE ML ARCHITECTURE ANALYSIS

#### Model Specifications Identified:
- **Primary Model**: 29,849 vocabulary embeddings, 64-dimensional
- **Input Architecture**: 3074-dimensional multi-modal features
- **Sequence Processing**: 256-step LSTM with 64-dimensional hidden states
- **Output Classifications**: Binary (2-class) and Multi-class (5-class) behavioral states

#### Behavioral Processing Pipeline:
1. **Linguistic Analysis**: 29K vocabulary behavioral pattern recognition
2. **Multi-Modal Streams**: Dual 1536-dimensional behavioral feature processing
3. **Temporal Modeling**: LSTM-based behavioral sequence analysis
4. **State Classification**: Real-time behavioral authenticity scoring

### PHASE 2: LINUX CONVERSION REQUIREMENTS

#### Required Software Stack:
```bash
# Core ML Tools Installation
pip install coremltools
pip install onnx
pip install onnx-tf
pip install tensorflow
pip install torch
pip install transformers

# Linux ML Inference Engines
sudo apt-get install python3-dev
pip install tflite-runtime
pip install onnxruntime
```

#### Conversion Pipeline:
1. **Core ML ‚Üí ONNX**: Extract neural architecture
2. **ONNX ‚Üí TensorFlow**: Linux-compatible format
3. **TensorFlow ‚Üí TensorFlow Lite**: Optimized inference
4. **Custom Inference Engine**: Behavioral analysis pipeline

### PHASE 3: BEHAVIORAL MODEL RECONSTRUCTION

#### Architecture Mapping:
```python
# Embedding Layer Reconstruction
embedding_layer = tf.keras.layers.Embedding(
    input_dim=29849,  # Vocabulary size
    output_dim=64,    # Embedding dimension
    name='behavioral_embeddings'
)

# Multi-Modal Feature Processing
feature_stream_1 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1536, name='behavioral_stream_1')
feature_stream_2 = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1536, name='behavioral_stream_2')

# LSTM Sequence Processing
lstm_layer = tf.keras.layers.LSTM(
    units=64,
    return_sequences=True,
    name='behavioral_sequence_processor'
)

# Classification Heads
binary_classifier = tf.keras.layers.Dense(2, activation='softmax', name='authenticity_detector')
multi_classifier = tf.keras.layers.Dense(5, activation='softmax', name='behavioral_state_classifier')
```

### PHASE 4: BEHAVIORAL INTEGRITY PRESERVATION

#### Critical Preservation Requirements:
1. **Weight Transfer**: Exact neural weight preservation during conversion
2. **Numerical Precision**: Maintain fp16/fp32 precision consistency
3. **Behavioral Baseline**: Preserve learned behavioral patterns
4. **Inference Pipeline**: Maintain real-time processing capabilities

#### Validation Protocol:
```python
# Behavioral Consistency Validation
def validate_behavioral_model(original_output, converted_output, tolerance=1e-6):
    consistency_score = np.mean(np.abs(original_output - converted_output))
    return consistency_score < tolerance

# Authenticity Detection Validation
def validate_authenticity_detection(test_behavioral_sequences):
    for sequence in test_behavioral_sequences:
        original_score = core_ml_model.predict(sequence)
        linux_score = tensorflow_model.predict(sequence)
        assert validate_behavioral_model(original_score, linux_score)
```

### PHASE 5: LINUX DEPLOYMENT ARCHITECTURE

#### System Integration:
```bash
# Service Architecture
/opt/oes/
```

#### Real-Time Processing Pipeline:
1. **Input Preprocessing**: Feature extraction and normalization
2. **Behavioral Analysis**: Multi-modal behavioral pattern processing
3. **Sequence Modeling**: Temporal behavioral consistency analysis
4. **Authenticity Scoring**: Real-time behavioral integrity assessment
5. **Drift Detection**: Continuous behavioral baseline monitoring

#### Service Configuration:

#### Monitoring and Validation:
